1.获取所有topic监控信息
---------------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topics
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取所有topic监控信息
- 参数 

|    字段    | 类型  | 备注  |
|:--------:|:---:|:---:|
|   page   | int |     |
| pageSize | int |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topics?page=0&pageSize=10
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"data":[],		"page":0,		"pageSize":10,		"pages":2,		"total":13	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
2.获取连接明细
--------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/connections/detail
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取连接明细
- 参数 

|  字段   |   类型   | 备注  |
|:-----:|:------:|:---:|
| topic | String | 主题  |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/jmq4_jmq2/connections/detail
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"clients":[],		"consumer":0,		"producer":0,		"total":0	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
3.获取partition监控信息
-----------------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/partition/:partition
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取partition监控信息
- 参数 

|    字段     |   类型   |    备注     |
|:---------:|:------:|:---------:|
|   topic   | String |    主题     |
|    app    | String |    应用     |
| partition | short  | partition |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/jmq4_jmq2/app/jmq2To4/partition/0
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"app":"jmq2To4",		"deQueue":{			"avg":0.0,			"count":0,			"max":0.0,			"min":0.0,			"oneMinuteRate":0,			"size":0,			"totalSize":0,			"tp90":0.0,			"tp99":0.0		},		"enQueue":{			"avg":0.0,			"count":0,			"max":0.0,			"min":0.0,			"oneMinuteRate":0,			"size":0,			"totalSize":0,			"tp90":0.0,			"tp99":0.0		},		"partition":0,		"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
4.getWritableResult
-------------------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/writable
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 无
- 参数 无


示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/writable
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"jmqCode":"FW_TOPIC_NOT_EXIST",		"success":false	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
5.获取生产者信息
---------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/producer/partitionGroup/:partitionGroupId
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取生产者信息
- 参数 

|        字段        |   类型   | 备注  |
|:----------------:|:------:|:---:|
|      topic       | String |     |
|       app        | String |     |
| partitionGroupId |  int   |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/jmq4_jmq2/app/jmq2To4/producer/partitionGroup/0
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"app":"jmq2To4",		"enQueue":{			"avg":0.0,			"count":0,			"max":0.0,			"min":0.0,			"oneMinuteRate":0,			"size":0,			"totalSize":0,			"tp90":0.0,			"tp99":0.0		},		"partitionGroupId":0,		"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```

7.获取消费者信息
---------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/consumer/partition/:partition
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取消费者信息
- 参数 

|    字段     |   类型   | 备注  |
|:---------:|:------:|:---:|
|   topic   | String |     |
|    app    | String |     |
| partition | short  |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/jmq4_jmq2/app/jmq2To4/consumer/partition/0
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"app":"jmq2To4",		"deQueue":{			"avg":0.0,			"count":0,			"max":0.0,			"min":0.0,			"oneMinuteRate":0,			"size":0,			"totalSize":0,			"tp90":0.0,			"tp99":0.0		},		"partition":0,		"pending":{			"count":0		},		"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```

10.查找协调者
--------
- 接口路径 /monitor/coordinator/group/:groupId/detail
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 查找协调者
- 参数 

|   字段    |   类型   | 备注  |
|:-------:|:------:|:---:|
| groupId | String |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/coordinator/group/abc/detail
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"current":{			"address":"192.168.112.92:50088",			"backEndPort":50089,			"dataCenter":"UNKNOWN",			"id":1552304440,			"ip":"192.168.112.92",			"managerPort":50091,			"monitorPort":50090,			"nameserverPort":50092,			"port":50088,			"retryType":"RemoteRetry"		},		"partitionGroup":0,		"replicas":[],		"topic":{			"code":"__group_coordinators",			"fullName":"__group_coordinators",			"namespace":""		}	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```

15.thread safe
broker state 扩展信息
--------------------------------
- 接口路径 /monitor/broker/brokerStatExt
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 thread safe
broker state 扩展信息,扩展信息包含topic>app>partitionGroup>partition积压
and broker id
- 参数 

|    字段     |  类型  | 备注  |
|:---------:|:----:|:---:|
| timeStamp | long |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/broker/brokerStatExt?timeStamp=19395935
```
响应: 
```

16.获取消费者信息
----------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/consumer/partitions
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取消费者信息
- 参数 

|  字段   |   类型   | 备注  |
|:-----:|:------:|:---:|
| topic | String |     |
|  app  | String |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/jmq4_jmq2/app/jmq2To4/consumer/partitions
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":[		{			"app":"jmq2To4",			"deQueue":{				"avg":0.0,				"count":8643,				"max":0.0,				"min":0.0,				"oneMinuteRate":0,				"size":0,				"totalSize":843572,				"tp90":0.0,				"tp99":0.0			},			"partition":1,			"pending":{				"count":0			},			"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"		},		{			"app":"jmq2To4",			"deQueue":{				"avg":0.0,				"count":8003,				"max":0.0,				"min":0.0,				"oneMinuteRate":0,				"size":0,				"totalSize":782758,				"tp90":0.0,				"tp99":0.0			},			"partition":2,			"pending":{				"count":0			},			"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"		},		{			"app":"jmq2To4",			"deQueue":{				"avg":0.0,				"count":8072,				"max":0.0,				"min":0.0,				"oneMinuteRate":0,				"size":0,				"totalSize":789536,				"tp90":0.0,				"tp99":0.0			},			"partition":3,			"pending":{				"count":0			},			"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"		},		{			"app":"jmq2To4",			"deQueue":{				"avg":0.0,				"count":8111,				"max":0.0,				"min":0.0,				"oneMinuteRate":0,				"size":0,				"totalSize":793524,				"tp90":0.0,				"tp99":0.0			},			"partition":4,			"pending":{				"count":0			},			"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"		}	],	"message":"SUCCESS"}

17.获取生产者信息
----------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/producer
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取生产者信息
- 参数 

|  字段   |   类型   | 备注  |
|:-----:|:------:|:---:|
| topic | String |     |
|  app  | String |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/jmq4_jmq2/app/jmq2To4/producer
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"app":"jmq2To4",		"connections":0,		"enQueue":{			"avg":0.0,			"count":32824,			"max":0.0,			"min":0.0,			"oneMinuteRate":0,			"size":0,			"totalSize":3208902,			"tp90":0.0,			"tp99":0.0		},		"topic":"jmq4_jmq2"	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
18.获得协调者组成员
-----------
- 接口路径 /monitor/coordinator/namespace/:namespace/group/:groupId/members
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获得协调者组成员
- 参数 

|    字段     |   类型    | 备注  |
|:---------:|:-------:|:---:|
| namespace | String  |     |
|  groupId  | String  |     |
|   topic   | String  |     |
| isFormat  | boolean |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/coordinator/namespace/jmq/group/abc/members?topic=jmq4_jmq2&isFormat=true
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
19.获取所有生产topic监控信息
------------------
- 接口路径 /monitor/producers
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取所有生产topic监控信息
- 参数 

|    字段    | 类型  | 备注  |
|:--------:|:---:|:---:|
|   page   | int |     |
| pageSize | int |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/producers?page=0&pageSize=10
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"data":[],		"page":0,		"pageSize":10,		"pages":5,		"total":43	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
20.getReadableResult
--------------------
- 接口路径 /monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/readable
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 无
- 参数 无


示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/:topic/app/:app/readable
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"jmqCode":"FW_TOPIC_NOT_EXIST",		"success":false	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```

|    字段     |   类型   |    备注     |

```

22.获取连接明细

|  字段   |   类型   | 备注  |

```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/topic/jmq4_jmq2/consumer/connections/detail
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":{		"clients":[],		"consumer":0,		"producer":0,		"total":0	},	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```

24.获取broker信息
-------------
- 接口路径 /monitor/broker
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取broker信息
- 参数 无


示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/monitor/broker
```

74.裸接口
------
- 接口路径 /manage/store/file
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 裸接口
- 参数 

|    字段    |   类型   | 备注  |
|:--------:|:------:|:---:|
|   file   | String |     |
| position |  long  |     |
|  length  |  int   |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/manage/store/file?file=abc&position=0&length=100
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":"LENGTH(4): 0\nPARTITION(2): 0\nINDEX(8): 0\nTERM(4): 0\nMAGIC(2): 0\nSYS(2): 0\nPRIORITY(1): 00(0)\nCLIENT_IP(16): \n\tHex: 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 0x00 \n\tString: \u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\u0000\nCLIENT_TIMESTAMP(8): 0 (1970-01-01 08:00:00.000)\nSTORAGE_TIMESTAMP(4): 0 (1970-01-01 08:00:00.000)\nCRC(8): 0\nFLAG(2): 0\nBODY(0): \n\tHex: \n\tString: \nBIZ_ID(0): \n\tHex: \n\tString: \nPROPERTY(0): \n\tHex: \n\tString: \nEXPAND(0): \n\tHex: \n\tString: \nAPP(0): \n\tHex: \n\tString: \n",	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```

78.获取message，如果有积压消息返回积压，否则返回最后几条
---------------------------------
- 接口路径 /manage/topic/:topic/app/:app/message/view
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 获取message，如果有积压消息返回积压，否则返回最后几条
- 参数 

|  字段   |   类型   | 备注  |
|:-----:|:------:|:---:|
| topic | String |     |
|  app  | String |     |
| count |  int   |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/manage/topic/jmq4_jmq2/app/jmq2To4/message/view?count=10
```
响应: 
```

80.返回最大ack索引
------------
- 接口路径 /manage/topic/:topic/app/:app/partition/:partition/ack
- 请求类型 GET
- 功能描述 返回最大ack索引
- 参数 

|    字段     |   类型   | 备注  |
|:---------:|:------:|:---:|
|   topic   | String |     |
|    app    | String |     |
| partition | short  |     |
示例: 请求: 
```
curl -X GET http://192.168.112.99:50090/manage/topic/jmq4_jmq2/app/jmq2To4/partition/0/ack
```
响应: 
```
{	"code":200,	"data":31789,	"message":"SUCCESS"}
```
